---
title: "Plantronics DSP 500 USB Headphones"
date: 2009-02-23
forum: Multimedia Software
---

### Post by New_Linux_user on 2009-02-23
Members:

I just came from the Ubuntu Bug jam this weekend at Scale 7 and we got a start to resolve the operation of the USB headphones in Ubuntu 8.04. The following is a summary what has to be done:

We looked at the devices before and after plugging in the headphones.

Need to edit Udev rules file.

Instead of being 'zeroes', some devices were showing up as 'ones', which led to incorrect devices being used as output.

The following is the before text file from the terminal:

Can anybody please solve this problem. I would like to use the USB headphone as my listening device to hear music files, movies, video files from the web, as well as Internet radio music. With Windows is just a matter of selecting the output device and it works fine. I enjoy Ubuntu, but this issue limits it's use.

Sincerely,

Nilo

### Post by cariboo on 2009-02-23
You should be able to set the output to your headphones using System-->Administraiton-->Sound, instead of using your sound card set the output to the usb device. It should look something this:

```
046d:08da
```

The above is actually my webcam, but if I use the device id for the microphone, it works.

Jim

### Post by markbuntu on 2009-02-25
Well yes, that is exactly what it is for. 

If, after that, you are having any trouble with applications sharing sound devices there is a quick guide here for that

[http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=997506](http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=997506)

The more extensive troubleshooting and setup guide is here

[http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=843012](http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=843012)
